{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2022-03-14 16:15:05","updatedTime":"2022-03-14 16:15:05","title":"What is a Media Kit — and How to Make One [+ Press Kit Examples]","link":"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/media-kit-examples","description":"<p>Your competitor releases a new product or service. You offer something similar — but, of course, much better.</p>  \n<p>Then, suddenly, your competitor's product is <em>everywhere</em>. News articles, online reviews, best-of lists, buyers' guides, even TV segments.</p> \n<p>How is this happening? And your real question: why isn't it happening to <em>you</em>?</p> \n<p>To compete against your competitors, there's one thing you'll need in your wheelhouse: a media kit.</p> \n<p>Here, we'll explore what a media kit is, and how it can help you increase brand awareness and, ultimately, sales.</p> \n<p>Plus, how to make one for your own brand.</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/cs/ci/?pg=0adc0556-31bd-4bf1-924b-6a0e48a4bedb&amp;pid=53&amp;ecid=&amp;hseid=&amp;hsic=\"><img class=\"hs-cta-img \" style=\"border-width: 0px; /*hs-extra-styles*/; margin: 0 auto; display: block; margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px\" alt=\"Download Now: Free Media Kit Template\" src=\"https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/53/0adc0556-31bd-4bf1-924b-6a0e48a4bedb.png\" align=\"middle\"></a></p> \n<p>Media kits may live fully-online as responsive online <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/agency/perfect-press-page\"><span>press pages</span></a>. Or, businesses may choose to make their press kits available as static, downloadable resources, like a presentation deck.</p> \n<p>Whatever format you choose, this much is clear: businesses of all sizes benefit from having a professional, readily-accessible media kit. This vital resource is a key to the <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/what-is-earned-media-faqs\"><span>earned media coverage</span></a> all businesses covet — from massive Fortune 500 corporations all the way down to individual influencers and solopreneurs.</p> \n<p>A comprehensive media kit should include a description of the company or individual, contact information, social media statistics, case studies, information on partnerships and collaborations, and testimonials from past customers.</p> \n<p>Basically, it's all the information a journalist would need to feature your brand in a breaking news story — without the headache of a last-minute information request.</p> \n<h2 style=\"font-weight: normal;\">How to Make a Media Kit: What to Include</h2> \n<p>So, you want press coverage and partnerships (what brand doesn't?). And you understand how a media kit helps make this all possible. But how do you <em>make</em> a media kit?</p> \n<p>Here's some good news: most of the content and creative assets you need to create your press kit likely already exist.</p> \n<p>Key elements of a media kit include a bio or About Us page, social media statistics, case studies, partnerships and collaborations, and testimonials. To make it even easier for the press to cover your work, you'll want to include high-quality brand identity images (think both logos, and other brand images or product/service images).</p> \n<p>It's up to you to (1) find this information, (2) make it look spectacular, and (3) make it painfully easy to find on your site. The rumors you've heard about journalists and how overworked they are? Entirely true.</p> \n<p>To catch the attention of someone on tight deadlines with an internet full of story prospects, you're going to want to make this simple. Most brands choose a direct page name like \"Press\" or \"Media\" –– or, if they're really fancy, \"Newsroom\" –– and make it accessible directly from their homepage (often in the Footer).</p> \n<p>Even if you prioritize a web version, having a downloadable media kit or deck is worth the time investment. Some media users might prefer the traditional form of this resource, and it gives you the best opportunity to control your pitch and tailor content to all audiences.</p> \n<h3>Biography or About Us</h3> \n<p>Let's start with the star of your media kit: <em>you</em>. Here's where you introduce your name, your logo, your mission. Make sure your media kit design reinforces your overall brand identity, utilizing the colors, fonts, and other visual hallmarks set out in your branding guide.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://evernote.com/about-us\"><span>Evernote</span></a> goes all-out in this section, housing their press kit information within the broader \"About Us\" portion of their website. All the essentials for journalists and partners are there too, but the organization's values take center stage.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Media%20Kit_Evernote-min.png?width=1205&amp;name=Media%20Kit_Evernote-min.png\" alt=\"Evernote's media kit homepage\" width=\"1205\" style=\"width: 1205px;\"></p> \n<h3>Social Statistics</h3> \n<p>For social stats, you'll need to conduct a <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/customers/check-pulse-digital-strategy-social-media-audit\"><span>social media audit</span></a> or collect this data from whoever manages your social channels. Remember your audience for the press kit: media and PR professionals.</p> \n<blockquote> \n <p>Your media kit needs to effectively pitch your brand to people who specialize in getting people's attention. So show them you're capable of sparking conversation — and show them there's <em>already</em> an audience eager for stories about you and your work.</p> \n</blockquote> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/help/brand_assets\"><span>Kickstarter</span></a> puts a unique stamp on this section of their media kit page, highlighting a few top metrics that show massive engagement with their service.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Media%20Kit_Kickstarter-min.png?width=2138&amp;name=Media%20Kit_Kickstarter-min.png\" alt=\"Kickstarter's media kit social media statistics\" width=\"2138\" style=\"width: 2138px;\"></p> \n<p>Media kits aimed at partnerships and collaborations should prioritize <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/vanity-metrics-to-stop-measuring-and-better-alternatives\"><span>engagement rates and similar actionable metrics</span></a> alongside the bread-and-butter statistics like follower counts. Savvy marketers want to partner with brands and influencers that move people to action.</p> \n<p>[Note: If you are a HubSpot Social user, you can use <a href=\"https://knowledge.hubspot.com/social-media-user-guide-v2/how-to-use-the-social-reports-tool\"><span>Reports</span></a> to analyze the performance of your social posts and determine how well your social media efforts are performing.]</p> \n<h3 style=\"font-weight: bold;\">Partnerships and Case Studies</h3> \n<p>This section is your chance to let past partnerships and brand collaborations speak for themselves. Let the old adage \"<em>show; don't tell</em>\" be your guide here. Featuring the right partnerships –– either via logos or through short case studies –– is a subtle but powerful tool for positioning your brand.</p> \n<p>International football influencers <a href=\"http://thef2.com/campaigns/\"><span>The F2</span></a> highlight past campaigns, putting reputable brand names and logos front-and-center. They also note key engagement statistics for these campaigns</p> \n<h3><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Media%20Kit_TheF2%20Influencer%20Campaigns%20MLS-min.png?width=1318&amp;name=Media%20Kit_TheF2%20Influencer%20Campaigns%20MLS-min.png\" alt=\"F2's media kit homepage\" width=\"1318\" style=\"width: 1318px;\"></h3> \n<h3 style=\"font-weight: bold;\">Testimonials</h3> \n<p>Testimonials are another great way to <em>show</em> media professionals the impact and effectiveness of your brand or product.</p> \n<p>Keep this section succinct: just a single testimonial should suffice. Only a few lines of text (even just a single short quote) and a single related image gets the point across, lending your pitch greater credibility thanks to <a href=\"https://www.forbes.com/sites/jaysondemers/2015/02/19/the-importance-of-social-validation-in-online-marketing/#50f51463364d\"><span>social validation</span></a>.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://briogeohair.com/pages/press\"><span>Briogeo</span></a> does a fantastic job highlighting testimonials on its Press &amp; Buzz page, right below the rewards section for easy access:<br><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/briogeo.png?width=1388&amp;name=briogeo.png\" alt=\"briogeo's media kit homepage with testimonials\" width=\"1388\" style=\"width: 1388px;\"></p> \n<h3 style=\"font-weight: bold;\">Visual Assets (Downloadables)</h3> \n<p>Your media kit isn't a style guide, but it should pull in the most essential elements of your visual brand. Want your logo and that slick product screenshot to display correctly?</p> \n<p>Provide exactly the images and files you want featured. Have a killer data visualization, infographic, or product video? Include that, too.</p> \n<p>Journalists will especially appreciate portraits of your management team. They're most likely to cover stories involving people, so show them the people they'll want to write about.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.birchbox.com/press/news\"><span>Birchbox</span></a> makes this easy. They highlight \"Press Materials\" and link to a short but comprehensive set of resources. Having everything in well-organized cloud folders is a nice touch –– especially for those browsing on mobile.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/HkoNrtUC4K3mBp4EB3E9XjtDt0rxF9XvAI3jHPHpVBNd8KLmbSTOaAMxdjuKs7_8SOaeSlxyN3PoIjhGfMUbsLwWgoLm0YSNjiCo3_pimDHDQ4nQ-st0Dszh1DE1E4RECkDWh1Ec\" width=\"672\" height=\"277\" alt=\"birchbox's media kit homepage\"></p> \n<p>Without downloading or unzipping a large batch of images, visitors can quickly confirm you have visual assets to make their publication look good. Remember, the audience for your media kit is especially busy and juggling lots of competing priorities. Jump to the top of their \"potential posts\" pile by making their job as easy and painless as possible.</p> \n<p>(Added bonus: your external media resources are easily updated –– sparing you anxiety about outdated media kits and image files misrepresenting your brand.)</p> \n<h2>Media Kit Design</h2> \n<p>Now that you know what to include in your media kit, you might be wondering how to put all of that valuable information together so that it’s navigable and easy to understand. You’ll do this through a table of contents.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>The way your table of contents looks can vary depending on how you design your media kit. On Slack’s website, its media kit has a table of contents that features summaries of each section with hyperlinks that bring users to a separate page, as shown in the image below.&nbsp;</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/slack%20website.jpg?width=1480&amp;name=slack%20website.jpg\" alt=\"slack website media kit table of contents\" width=\"1480\" style=\"width: 1480px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center; font-size: 13px;\"><a href=\"https://slack.com/media-kit\" style=\"font-style: italic;\">Image Source</a></p> \n<p>If you download Slack’s media kit as a PDF, the table of contents lists a page number for each section, so viewers can quickly scroll to the page they need or type the page number into the search bar.&nbsp;</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/slack%20image%202.jpeg?width=1650&amp;name=slack%20image%202.jpeg\" alt=\"slack downloadable media kit table of contents\" width=\"1650\" style=\"width: 1650px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center; font-size: 13px;\"><a href=\"https://slack.com/media-kit\" style=\"font-style: italic;\">Image Source</a></p> \n<p>Regardless of how you present your kit, it needs to be designed for ease of access. Aim to create distinct sections for the content you’re including, and create a form of navigation that helps those making inquiries quickly find what they need.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Let’s go over some high-quality examples of media kits that you can use for inspiration when creating one for your business.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>Media Kit Examples</h2> \n<h3>1. Hinge</h3> \n<p>Hinge, a dating app, has a straightforward and easy to navigate press kit that gives those doing media inquiries quick access to critical information, like internal press releases:</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/hinge%20image%201.jpg?width=2642&amp;name=hinge%20image%201.jpg\" alt=\"press kit example: hinge media kit\" width=\"2642\" style=\"width: 2642px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center; font-size: 13px;\"><a href=\"https://hinge.co/press/\" style=\"font-style: italic;\">Image Source</a></p> \n<p>As well as external news articles, employee profiles, business background, and image downloads (logo, screenshots, etc.).</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/hinge%20image%202.png?width=2752&amp;name=hinge%20image%202.png\" alt=\"press kit example: hinge media kit downloadables\" width=\"2752\" style=\"width: 2752px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center; font-size: 13px;\"><a href=\"https://hinge.co/press/\" style=\"font-style: italic;\">Image Source</a></p> \n<h3>2. Spotify</h3> \n<p><a href=\"https://downloads.ctfassets.net/ziwa9xqm84y1/4FeDT9GwCmVOj2k0vyqr5O/f2adf8dc6bd540a310af13ab77812da1/Media_Kit_Q1_2020_-_US.pdf\">Spotify </a>has a unique media kit, namely one that supports one of its key features — Streaming Intelligence. Media and other parties can read through the kit, understand the specifics of the tool, how it works, performance stats, as well as partnerships with notable sources that support its effectiveness.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Spotify shows us that general press kits are great for your business to have, but are also relevant for things like product launches or specific business tools.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3>3. Delta Airlines</h3> \n<p><a href=\"https://docs.google.com/document/d/1JH0wBgARtMmTUDTNjWa3v5i1dc5UXPCDk5jd-tBRsGA/edit#heading=h.ox66b43gonaq\">Delta Airlines</a>’ press kit is hosted on its website and contains all of the elements you’d expect from one. As it is such a large company, each section of the press kit is on a different site page that users navigate to by clicking a hyperlink.&nbsp;</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delta%20image%201.jpg?width=2502&amp;name=delta%20image%201.jpg\" alt=\"media kit example: delta press kit table of contents\" width=\"2502\" style=\"width: 2502px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center; font-size: 13px;\"><a href=\"https://news.delta.com/\" style=\"font-style: italic;\">Image Source</a></p> \n<p>If you click on a link for, say, Awards and Recognitions, you land on a page that features noteworthy recognitions about Delta and the service it offers.&nbsp;</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delta%202.jpg?width=409&amp;name=delta%202.jpg\" alt=\"media kit example: delta press kit statistics\" width=\"409\" style=\"width: 409px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<p style=\"font-size: 13px; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://news.delta.com/delta-worlds-most-awarded-airline\" style=\"font-style: italic;\">Image Source</a></p> \n<p>Now you know the <em>what </em>and the <em>how </em>of creating a media kit to garner beneficial coverage for your brand. <a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/business-templates/media-kit\">Click here to download our free media kit template and get started.</a></p> \n<p>And go ahead, give yourself a pat on the back when that Features story comes out. 16:15:05","updatedTime":"2022-03-14 16:15:05","title":"Which Instagram Story Formats Really Engage Viewers [New Research]","link":"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/instagram-story-formats","description":"<p>In 2021, Instagram reported over <a href=\"https://www.omnicoreagency.com/instagram-statistics/#:~:text=Instagram%20Stories%20statistics,after%20seeing%20it%20in%20Stories.\">500 million users</a> viewed Stories.&nbsp;</p>  \n<p>Since <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/instagram-stories\">launching in 2016</a>, the Stories feature alone has made Instagram more popular than other Story and mobile video platform competitors including <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/snapchat-discover-examples\">Snapchat</a>, <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/what-is-tiktok\">TikTok</a>, and its owner's own platform: <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/preferred-story-platforms\">Facebook Stories</a>.</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/cs/ci/?pg=55f44553-d63a-43bd-8957-63ac11fbcdb3&amp;pid=53&amp;ecid=&amp;hseid=&amp;hsic=\"><img class=\"hs-cta-img \" style=\"border-width: 0px; /*hs-extra-styles*/; margin: 0 auto; display: block; margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px\" alt=\"Access Now: 22 Free Business Instagram Templates\" src=\"https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/53/55f44553-d63a-43bd-8957-63ac11fbcdb3.png\" align=\"middle\"></a></p> \n<p>&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Even if you've already published a handful of branded Stories, you still might want to up your game by making them even more engaging. After all, Stories can provide great benefits related to <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/instagram-stories\">audience engagement, brand awareness, and even purchase-related conversions</a>.</p> \n<p>Despite the growing number of benefits that Instagram Stories offers brands, crafting good content still takes time, energy, and brainstorming. Even when you put your best efforts into creating a Story, you might still find that it falls flat, sees a high drop-off, or shows other signs of low engagement.</p> \n<p>As you build your social media content strategy for 2022, you might be asking yourself, \"What type of Instagram Story format do people actually engage with?\"</p> \n<p>In this post, I'll highlight what consumers said about their favorite Instagram Story formats, the trends marketers are noticing, and show you examples along the way.</p> \n<h2>Which Formats Marketers Are Leveraging [HubSpot Blog Data]</h2> \n<p>The HubSpot Blog surveyed over 1,000 marketers to learn more about their marketing strategies in 2022. According to this survey, 78% of marketers leverage Instagram Stories in their roles. Of those who use Instagram Stories, 43% post on behalf of their brand multiple times per week. The marketers in this survey note audience viewership of Instagram Stories declines after four to six Instagram Story pages.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>According to the marketers we surveyed, here are the most common Instagram Story types subjects that result in the greatest ROI.</p> \n<h3>Content That Reflects Brand Values</h3> \n<p>Per the HubSpot Blog survey, 18% of marketers indicated Instagram Story content that reflected their brand’s values produced the greatest ROI. Considering <a href=\"https://smallbiztrends.com/2020/02/brand-values-alignment.html\"><span>71% of consumers</span></a> want to buy from brands that align with their personal values, this piece of data isn’t surprising.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>When companies are upfront about their core values related to topics such as diversity, inclusion, sustainability, and human rights, buyers are able to quickly determine a brand’s stance on a particular topic.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Similarly, it’s important that consumers know why your brand exists, and how you can serve them. Regularly incorporating your company’s mission and vision into your content can also help your audience feel more connected to your brand.</p> \n<h3>Product-Focused Content</h3> \n<p>Consumers want to see your product in action! Whether it is through regular demonstrations by your team, user-generated content from other happy customers, or positive reviews, product-related content can deliver positive results. When crafting Instagram Stories, find creative ways to present your products that appeal to your audience.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3>Interactive Content</h3> \n<p>On Instagram Stories, interactive frames have a specific call-to-action or way viewers can get involved from within the app. This often includes using Instagram’s Poll or Quiz sticker, inviting users to share a specific piece of content themselves, or a game. Here’s an example from <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/fentybeauty/\">@fentybeauty</a>, who used Instagram’s slide feature to poll their audience.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Interactive-Content-Example.jpg?width=200&amp;name=Interactive-Content-Example.jpg\" alt=\"Instagram Story Format: an example of an interactive Instagram Story\" width=\"200\" style=\"width: 200px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<h3>Trendy Content</h3> \n<p>Trend-related content entails coverage of a recent cultural moment or news story. This type of content can range from informative (breaking news) to humorous (posting a meme related to a recent event). Trendy content is well-suited for Instagram Stories because of it is best consumed quickly and while relevant. Unlike a feed post that can take days to reach an audience, the 24-hour period an Instagram Story is live can be a great place to share content that is only relevant for a short period of time.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Now that we know what content marketers are prioritizing in Instagram Stories, let’s look at what formats consumers prefer and engage with most often.</p> \n<h2>Which Format Consumers Are Actually Watching</h2> \n<p>While some brands and users post Stories focused purely on interactive features, others might post visual storytelling content such as short narratives or longer video stories that feel more like documentaries.</p> \n<p>But, which one of the many Instagram Story formats is most intriguing to people? To get to the bottom of which Story style is most engaging, I surveyed 350 people using <a href=\"https://luc.id/\">Lucid</a> software to learn more about their favorite Story formats, sound preferences, and ideal Story length.</p> \n<p>I asked consumers, \"Which Instagram Story are you most likely to tap all the way through until the end?\"</p> \n<p>At this point, you may have your own predictions of how people might have voted. While research says that interactive stickers, such as Quizzes, Polls, or Questions are highly engaging, you might also be thinking about the times you've tapped through an influencer or brand's behind-the-scenes videos via their Story. So which, ultimately did people choose?</p> \n<p>Stories centered around Quiz or Poll stickers were one of the most popular formats with 15% of the votes. However, 35% of consumers <em>actually</em> prefer short narratives with a mix of photos, text, and videos.</p> \n<div>\n <img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hubfs/Instagram%20Story%20Formats.png\" alt=\"Which types of Instagram Stories do you tap all the way through?\">\n</div> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><em>Data Source: </em><a href=\"http://luc.id/\">Lucid Software</a></p> \n<h3>Short Narrative Stories</h3> \n<p>Short narratives are basically articles translated for a more visual audience. They rely on brief paragraphs and bullet points of text, accompanied by related visuals, to tell a story in a few cohesive short slides. Here's a great example of a short story that swipes up to a longer piece of web content from <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/instagram-story-examples\">Harvard Business Review</a>:</p> \n<div>\n <img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Instagram%20Story%20Formats-3.png?width=600&amp;name=Instagram%20Story%20Formats-3.png\" alt=\"Harvard Business Review Instagram Story\" width=\"600\" style=\"width: 600px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\">\n</div> \n<p>This strategy is a great way to get more eyes on your blog content without asking people to leave the Instagram app.</p> \n<p>Aside from informing your audience of a topic related to your industry, you can also take a note from HBR and other publishers by using Stories as a traffic generator. In the example above, HBR — which has a verified account — has adapted a long-form article into a short Story and included the full post at the end as a swipe-up link.</p> \n<p>With this tactic, the Instagram Story serves as a teaser as viewers who are very interested in the topic can swipe up to read more about it on HBR.org.</p> \n<h3>Quiz or Poll-Centered Stories</h3> \n<p>Another strong Story format uses Quiz or Poll stickers. Essentially, these Stories feel like they are just created to quiz the viewer by including the Quiz sticker on most pages, or brands can leverage Stories with polls primarily on each page to get their audience's insights on a topic.</p> \n<p>These Stories are intriguing and entertaining to viewers because it allows them to test themselves and learn about a new topic interactively, or vote in a poll and see what other audiences think about a certain topic or theme. Here's an example of an interactive Story from HubSpot which centered around a Poll-styled quiz and revealed the answers at the end.</p> \n<div>\n <img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Instagram%20Story%20Formats-4.png?width=600&amp;name=Instagram%20Story%20Formats-4.png\" alt=\"HubSpot Poll Instagram Story\" width=\"600\" style=\"width: 600px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\">\n</div> \n<p>While you can also use an actual Quiz sticker, which will immediately tell viewers quiz questions, HubSpot's strategy also works as it allows viewers to get a glimpse at what others guessed and see a rundown of the actual answers at the end. This might keep viewers engaged, entertained, and in the Story for longer if they know that there will be a payoff on the last page.</p> \n<p>While fewer people voted for Stories centered around <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/instagram-questions\">Question stickers</a>, this feature could still be a great feature to experiment with as it can help you interact with and learn more about your audience in a more open-ended way that Polls.</p> \n<p>Here's an example of a Question sticker in a HubSpot Story. After this page, the Story went on to share the answers that viewers submitted.</p> \n<div>\n <img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Instagram%20Story%20Formats-11.png?width=200&amp;name=Instagram%20Story%20Formats-11.png\" alt=\"HubSpot Questions INstagram Story\" width=\"200\" style=\"width: 200px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\">\n</div> \n<p>Although open-ended questions seem like a great way to learn about and interact with your audience, keep in mind that viewers will need to take time to fill out answers rather than simply tapping on a Poll or Quiz sticker. This means that if your audience isn't as interested in the topic or question, you might run into issues getting responses.</p> \n<p>If you'd like to learn more about how to use and leverage the Instagram Questions sticker in your Stories, check out <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/instagram-questions\">this helpful guide</a> which includes examples of brands that used the feature successfully.</p> \n<h3>Demos and Tutorials</h3> \n<p>Brands can also leverage tutorials and demos, which was the fifth most popular Story style. This tactic might be especially helpful if you're interested in ecommerce or purchase-related conversions as a <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/video-marketing\">growing number of people prefer to learn more about products via video.</a> Here's an example of a <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/social-media-product-research\">tutorial from Kylie Cosmetics</a>, where CEO Kylie Jenner puts on a new lip liner from the brand.</p> \n<div>\n <img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Instagram%20Story%20Formats-8.png?width=200&amp;name=Instagram%20Story%20Formats-8.png\" alt=\"Kylie Cosmetics Instagram Story Tutorial\" width=\"200\" style=\"width: 200px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\">\n</div> \n<p>Story formats that include demos or tutorials can be advantageous to brands because it allows them to show off how their products work. Additionally, if you have <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/add-link-instagram-story\">over 10,000 followers or are a verified user</a>, you can link these Stories to your ecommerce site or a purchasing page for the products shown. This way, if a viewer is impressed by a tutorial or demo, they can simply swipe up to learn more about or purchase the product.</p> \n<h3>A Mix of Content</h3> \n<p>Because many people don't have a preference or prefer a mix of multiple elements in Instagram Stories, be sure to add a bit of variation to your content strategy. For example, brainstorm ways to add interactive features, such as Quiz or Poll stickers to narratives, tutorials, or other types of Story content. This will add an extra layer of engaging content to a Story that might already be interesting to viewers.</p> \n<p>Here's an example of a <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/instagram-story-examples\">Story from Starbucks</a> that mixes in storytelling and interactive stickers to announce the return of a popular seasonal beverage:</p> \n<div>\n <img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Instagram%20Story%20Formats-5.png?width=600&amp;name=Instagram%20Story%20Formats-5.png\" alt=\"Starbucks Instagram Story\" width=\"600\" style=\"width: 600px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\">\n</div> \n<h2>Other Instagram Story Formats</h2> \n<p>When it came to the Story styles with lower rankings, consumers were actually less interested in behind-the-scenes content, mini-documentaries, and Stories that center around customer testimonials.</p> \n<p>This might hint that marketers on these platforms might want to be thinking more creatively when launching content on Instagram Stories. Rather than just focusing on your product or customer testimonials, you might want to test out creating informative short narratives or interactive Stories that relate strongly to your brand. While this will engage Instagram audiences, it might also show off your company's expertise in its industry.</p> \n<p>While this poll deemed a few Story formats less engaging, I still encourage you to mix things up and experiment with some of these styles just in case they work for you. Here are a few to try.</p> \n<h3>Customer Testimonials</h3> \n<p>Although customer testimonials aren't as interesting to consumers, this doesn't mean that you should scratch them entirely. In fact, they're still a commonly used tactic in many brands and industries, despite consumer preferences. For example, a number of companies, like <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/instagram-story-examples\">Planet Fitness</a>, have built their strategy around testimonials. Here's an example:</p> \n<div>\n <img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Instagram%20Story%20Formats-7.png?width=600&amp;name=Instagram%20Story%20Formats-7.png\" alt=\"Planet Fitness Instagram Story\" width=\"600\" style=\"width: 600px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\">\n</div> \n<p>In the above scenario, the customer testimonial strategy works for Planet Fitness because it helps gym prospects feel less intimidated and more motivated to take on physical fitness after seeing a customer's success story.</p> \n<h3>Behind-the-Scenes Stories</h3> \n<p>No, behind-the-scenes Stories don't necessarily talk about your product front and center, but they can give prospects an idea of what your company is like, the inner workings of your industry, and a look at the staff that customers could work with.</p> \n<p>Behind-the-scenes videos allow you to show off how hardworking or relatable your business might be, which might make viewers feel more comfortable working with you.</p> \n<p>One example of a brand that uses this technique is the <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/instagram-story-examples\">NBA</a>. The basketball league regularly <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/instagram-story-examples\">shares videos of professional basketball players behind the scenes</a> at games or celebrations. In the image below, they shared an Instagram Story video of basketball players taking a photo with the rapper Drake:</p> \n<div>\n <img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Instagram%20Story%20Formats-1.png?width=200&amp;name=Instagram%20Story%20Formats-1.png\" alt=\"NBA Instagram Story\" width=\"200\" style=\"width: 200px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\">\n</div> \n<h3>Mini-Documentaries</h3> \n<p>Like narrative-style Instagram content, mini-documentaries tell journalistic stories that are slightly more complex and primarily centered on video -- like a documentary that you tap through.</p> \n<p>These are often higher-quality and incredibly informative, so they are more prominently used by publishers such as National Geographic. Here's just the beginning of a long documentary-styled Story where NatGeo visits NASA's offices to uncover facts about the first moon landing:</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-3750.png?width=600&amp;name=image-3750.png\" width=\"600\" style=\"width: 600px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\" alt=\"NASA Instagram Story\"></p> \n<p>If you're a small to medium-sized business that's just ramping up your Instagram strategy, you might want to stick to a short narrative Story, like the ones noted at the beginning of this post. These will allow you to similarly show a combination of videos, photos, and text without as much production time and effort. However, if you're a content creator or feel like covering an event or newsworthy topic in your industry might boost brand awareness, you might want to experiment with this longer-form, in-depth visual storytelling style.</p> \n<h2>Ideal Story Length</h2> \n<p>For years, social media managers have been trying to determine how long the perfect Instagram Story should be. This has been such a major question that marketing blogs and publications have <a href=\"https://medium.com/swlh/the-biggest-instagram-stories-research-study-done-to-date-552662f6952b\">done further research on the matter</a>.</p> \n<p>If you're a small to medium-sized business marketer, Story length is a valid thing to consider, especially if you have low time or resources. While you ideally want to engage people with low dropoff throughout your entire Story, you might not want to spend time making incredibly long pieces of content with multiple pages if you know people in your industry usually only tap through a small number of pages.</p> \n<p>So, what exactly is a good Story length? To get some added insight on this, I surveyed the 350 consumers and asked them, \"On average, how many pages of an Instagram Story will you tap through before swiping out?\"</p> \n<p>Before looking at the results, you might think \"The ideal Story should be as short as possible,\" simply because it's content on a fast-paced social media platform. But, then, you might also remember that a number of publications, like Harvard Business Publishing and The Washington Post have leveraged Stories as a way to share long-form content.</p> \n<p>So, which approach is right and which is wrong?'</p> \n<p>It seems that there are solid themes in ideal Story length, however, there still might not be an ideal number of pages in this type of content.</p> \n<p>According to the poll, 63% of consumers will tap through six pages or less, with 34% saying they tap through four to six pages on average. This data aligns with the feedback we got from marketers through our HubSpot Blog survey. However, more than one-third of consumers will tap through stories with more than seven pages, with 20% saying they'll tap through 10 or more.</p> \n<div>\n <img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Instagram%20Story%20Formats-6.png?width=600&amp;name=Instagram%20Story%20Formats-6.png\" alt=\"How long should an Instagram Story be?\" width=\"600\" style=\"width: 600px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\">\n</div> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><em>Data Source: </em><a href=\"http://luc.id/\">Lucid Software</a></p> \n<p>The results above are similar to research published by Buffer which noted that Stories made up of <a href=\"https://medium.com/swlh/the-biggest-instagram-stories-research-study-done-to-date-552662f6952b\">seven or fewer pages are the most engaging</a>. However, the fact that a large chunk of Lucid respondents will watch beyond seven pages hints that you might not need to shrink down your content to ensure that it's seen.</p> \n<p>When determining the best Story length for your audience, we encourage you to consider the age group of your audience, the type of topics they engage with, and how fast-paced their lifestyles might be. If you have an idea for a great topic that your audience will love and is compatible with interactive Story features, you might be able to get away with a longer Story.</p> \n<p>If you have a topic that you worry might feel dry or too complex to explain on Stories, you might want to format this as a smaller Story with a <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/instagram-swipe-up-removal\">sticker linked to longer-form content</a>.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>As you start posting regular Instagram Stories, you should also experiment with both long and short Stories. Then, look at the drop-off rate of each Story. If many people seem to drop out of one long story but not another, this might be due to the topic or the writing rather than the length. However, if people regularly drop out of your longer-form Stories around a certain page number, you might want to limit your Story content to that number of pages.</p> \n<h2>Telling an Engaging Visual Story</h2> \n<p>Regardless of what topic you're publishing a Story about, or which format you decide on using, make sure it informs the audience about something they care about, provides entertainment value, and highlights your brand's credibility in your industry.</p> \n<p>If you're unsure about how you can leverage Instagram Stories to better market your brand, it can be helpful to look at examples from similar companies in your industry.&nbsp;</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" 16:15:05","updatedTime":"2022-03-14 16:15:05","title":"How To Create a Google Sheets Drop-down Menu","link":"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/google-sheets-drop-down","description":"<p>A lot of the data you <span style=\"font-weight: normal;\">enter </span>into your <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/google-sheets?_ga=2.201506711.729508953.1645129030-378566612.1645129030\">Google Sheets</a>&nbsp;tables may be repetitive, like tracking whether an influencer you’ve reached out to for a partnership has agreed to working with you or not.</p>  \n<p>It can get tedious to go in and type each yes or no as time goes on, which is where a critical tool, the drop-down list, becomes your best friend.</p> \n<p>In this post, we’ll go over how to add a drop-down list to your own Google Sheets data set to help save time.</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/cs/ci/?pg=e7cd3f82-cab9-4017-b019-ee3fc550e0b5&amp;pid=53&amp;ecid=&amp;hseid=&amp;hsic=\"><img class=\"hs-cta-img \" style=\"border-width: 0px; /*hs-extra-styles*/; margin: 0 auto; display: block; margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px\" alt=\"→ Access Now: Google Sheets Templates [Free Kit]\" src=\"https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/53/e7cd3f82-cab9-4017-b019-ee3fc550e0b5.png\" align=\"middle\"></a></p> \n<h2>How to Add a Drop-down List in Google Sheets</h2> \n<p>As mentioned above, a drop-down list can help you easily change elements of a cell when the content is repetitive.</p> \n<p>The example data set for this walkthrough (as shown in the image below) is tracking the progress of marketing campaigns on different channels and the stage they’re in; not yet started, in progress, or completed. I want to create a drop-down menu so I can easily go in and change the status of the campaign as time goes on.</p> \n<p><img alt=\"table in google sheets with a drop-down menu\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/google%20sheets%20drop%20down-Feb-17-2022-08-18-52-02-PM.png?width=553&amp;name=google%20sheets%20drop%20down-Feb-17-2022-08-18-52-02-PM.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 553px;\" title=\"\" width=\"553\"></p> \n<p>Before going through the steps, it might be helpful to see what a drop-down menu looks like so you can contextually understand each instruction. The gif below shows a final drop-down menu and how it applies to the sample data set.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/completed%20drop%20down%20menu.png?width=571&amp;name=completed%20drop%20down%20menu.png\" alt=\"completed drop down menu\" width=\"571\" style=\"width: 571px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<p>Let’s go over how to add a drop-down list to your Sheet.</p> \n<p>1. In the toolbar header, click <em>Data</em>.</p> \n<p>2. In the drop-down menu, as shown in the image below, select <em>Data validation</em>.</p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img alt=\"google sheets drop-down menu step 1: select data in the header toolbar\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/google%20sheets%20drop%20down-1.png?width=249&amp;name=google%20sheets%20drop%20down-1.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 249px;\" title=\"\" width=\"249\"></p> \n<p>3. In the <em>Data validation</em>&nbsp;dialog box, enter the range of cells you want to have a drop-down menu in <em>Cell range</em>. For this example, I’m entering B2:B10 for cells 2-10 in column B.</p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img alt=\"google sheets drop-down menu step 3: add your cell range\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/google%20sheets%20drop%20down-2.png?width=439&amp;name=google%20sheets%20drop%20down-2.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 439px;\" title=\"\" width=\"439\"></p> \n<p>4. The next step is to enter the data range that you want to be included in the drop-down menu. Select <em>List of items</em>, and add in your menu values. For this example, this is where I would input Not yet started, In progress, and Complete.</p> \n<p>Once you’ve entered your values, click save.</p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img alt=\"google sheets drop-down menu step 4: enter your list item criteria\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/google%20sheets%20drop%20down-4.png?width=509&amp;name=google%20sheets%20drop%20down-4.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" title=\"\" width=\"509\"></p> \n<p>5. Each of your cells should now have a clickable down arrow, as shown in the image below.</p> \n<p><img alt=\"google sheets drop-down menu arrows\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/google%20sheets%20drop%20down-Feb-17-2022-08-18-52-84-PM.png?width=579&amp;name=google%20sheets%20drop%20down-Feb-17-2022-08-18-52-84-PM.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 579px;\" title=\"\" width=\"579\"></p> \n<p>For the example table, I can click on each down arrow and change the status of my campaigns as time goes on.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/step%206-1.gif?width=569&amp;name=step%206-1.gif\" alt=\"step 6-1\" width=\"569\" style=\"width: 569px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<h2>How to Edit a Drop-down List in Google Sheets</h2> \n<p>If you need to make changes to your drop-down menu, the process is rather simple.</p> \n<p>1. In the toolbar header, click <em>Data</em>&nbsp;and then <em>Data validation</em>.</p> \n<p>2. In the <em>Data validation</em>&nbsp;dialogue box, simply input the changes you want to make. For example,</p> \n<ul> \n <li>If you want to change the items in your drop-down menu, navigate to <em>Criteria</em>, and make your desired changes.</li> \n <li>If you want to change the column the drop-down menu is in, change the cell numbers in <em>Cell range</em>.</li> \n <li>If you want to delete your drop-down menu altogether, select the column the menu is currently in and click <em>Remove validation</em>.</li> \n</ul> \n<p>Always click save after making all changes.</p> \n<h2>Color Code a Drop-down List in Google Sheets</h2> \n<p>Color coding is helpful when it comes to interpreting results at a glance. You can do this with your drop-down list by creating conditional formatting rules, and below we’ll explain how.</p> \n<p>1. Select the cells your drop-down menu is in and click <em>Format</em>.</p> \n<p>2. Select <em>Conditional formatting</em>&nbsp;from the dialogue box, as shown in the image below.</p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img alt=\"color code google sheets drop down menu step 2: click format in header toolbar\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/google%20sheets%20drop%20down-3.png?width=265&amp;name=google%20sheets%20drop%20down-3.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 265px;\" title=\"\" width=\"265\"></p> \n<p>3. In the <em>Conditional formatting rules</em>&nbsp;sidebar on the right-hand side of your screen, navigate to the <em>Format rules</em>&nbsp;section.</p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img alt=\"color code google sheets drop down menu step 3: select format rules\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/google%20sheets%20drop%20down.png?width=247&amp;name=google%20sheets%20drop%20down.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 247px;\" title=\"\" width=\"247\"></p> \n<p>4. In the <em>Format cells</em>&nbsp;if menu, select <em>Text contains…</em></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img alt=\"color code google sheets drop down menu step 4: select text contains\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/google%20sheets%20drop%20down-Feb-17-2022-08-18-53-08-PM.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" title=\"\"></p> \n<p>5. Enter the first element in your drop-down list that you want color-coded. In the image below, I’ve entered Completed<em>&nbsp;</em>as my value and set the color to Green.</p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/google%20sheets%20drop%20down-Feb-17-2022-08-18-52-29-PM.png?height=343&amp;name=google%20sheets%20drop%20down-Feb-17-2022-08-18-52-29-PM.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" title=\"\" height=\"343\"></p> \n<p>6. To set a color for each of your list items, select <em>+ Add another rule </em>and repeat step 5 for each value. For my chart, I’ve set In progress to Blue, and Not started to gray.</p> \n<p><img alt=\"color coded google sheets drop-down menu\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/google%20sheets%20drop%20down-Feb-17-2022-08-18-52-59-PM.png?width=624&amp;height=292&amp;name=google%20sheets%20drop%20down-Feb-17-2022-08-18-52-59-PM.png\" style=\"margin-left: 0.00px;\" title=\"\" width=\"624\" height=\"292\"></p> \n<p>7. After you set each of your rules, changing the drop-down menu item to a different value will automatically change it to the correct color. For example, if I change Not yet started to In progress, it turns from gray to blue.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/step%2019.gif?width=600&amp;name=step%2019.gif\" alt=\"step 19\" width=\"600\" style=\"width: 600px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<p>Once you’ve created your drop-down menu and color-coded it for easy interpretation, you can continue to track the progress of your different marketing activities and save time while doing so.</p> \n<p></p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" 16:15:05","updatedTime":"2022-03-14 16:15:05","title":"TikTok Trends B2B and B2C Marketers Should Watch in 2022","link":"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/tiktok-trends","description":"<p>According to Hubspot Blog Research, 44% of marketers currently leverage TikTok.</p>  \n<p>As the <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/short-form-video-trends?_ga=2.168827554.2098374504.1645840618-1209778046.1645840618\">short-form video</a> platform continues to grow, some brands are struggling to figure out where they fit in. In fact, a 2022 <a href=\"https://invideo.io/blog/tiktok-brand-marketing-report/\">report by InVideo </a>shows that around 50% of brands like Google and IKEA still aren’t leveraging the platform.</p> \n<p>In this article, we’ll cover the top <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/what-is-tiktok\">TikTok</a> trends at a brand marketing level, how to find trends on the platform, and tips for joining them.</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/cs/ci/?pg=2c7242e4-ad54-4f63-8627-a15aa6a2ea50&amp;pid=53&amp;ecid=&amp;hseid=&amp;hsic=\"><img class=\"hs-cta-img \" style=\"border-width: 0px; /*hs-extra-styles*/; margin: 0 auto; display: block; margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px\" alt=\"Free Ebook: The Marketer's Guide to TikTok for Business [Download Now]\" src=\"https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/53/2c7242e4-ad54-4f63-8627-a15aa6a2ea50.png\" align=\"middle\"></a></p> \n<h2>Top TikTok Trends</h2> \n<h3>1. More businesses are exploring the platform.</h3> \n<p>According to HubSpot Blog Research, TikTok is the number one platform marketers are increasing their investments in for 2022.</p> \n<p>For a long time, businesses didn’t take TikTok seriously. They saw it as a platform for Gen-Z to make short, funny videos.</p> \n<p>However, when its popularity (and user growth) peaked in 2020, businesses gave it a second look.</p> \n<p>Today, marketers say it’s the fourth most effective social media platform behind Instagram, FB, and YouTube. That puts it ahead of established platforms like Twitter and Pinterest.</p> \n<p>What makes TikTok special is its ability to build community. In fact, 78% of users agree that the best brands on TikTok are ones that work together with users, according to <a href=\"https://ads.tiktok.com/business/creativecenter/whats_next.html\">TikTok’s 2021 \"What’s Next\" report</a>.</p> \n<p>The report also found 67% of users feel inspired to shop even when they weren’t originally planning to.</p> \n<p>Brands are starting to realize that while users may first go on the platform for funny videos, they stay for the authenticity and community building – which are great pillars for brand loyalty.</p> \n<h3>2. TikTok users are consuming less of other content.</h3> \n<p>What would you do with your audience’s undivided attention?</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/business/en/blog/time-well-spent\">According to Kantar research</a>, 46% of users engage with content on the platform without any other distractions.</p> \n<p>More specifically, 41% of<a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/tiktok-influencer-agency-tips-for-creating-gen-z-content\"> Gen Z TikTok users</a> say they listen to fewer podcasts after joining TikTok and 33% say they watch less TV.</p> \n<p>This is an incredible opportunity for social media marketers to capitalize on this attention to reel in their audience and drive more engagement.</p> \n<h3>3. Sounds are more important than hashtags.</h3> \n<p>On no other social media platform does sound play such a pivotal role.</p> \n<p>88% of people on TikTok report that the sound on the platform is central to the overall app experience, according to TikTok’s \"What’s Next\" report.</p> \n<p>The report also revealed that sounds saw 47% higher video view rates on 2021 from the \"For You\" page when compared to hashtags.</p> \n<p>Furthermore, <a href=\"https://invideo.io/blog/tiktok-brand-marketing-report/\">Invideo’s TikTok Brand Marketing Report</a> found that 80% of the top videos had music, with upbeat songs being the most popular TikTok music choice by far.</p> \n<p>With this in mind, brands should prioritize the use of sounds when <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/when-to-post-tiktok\">posting on the platform</a>. While hashtags are effective in helping you reach your target audience, choosing the right sound will likely be more effective.</p> \n<h2>How to Find TikTok Trends</h2> \n<h3>1. The \"Discover\" Tab</h3> \n<p>One of the best ways to find trends on Tiktok is through the \"Discover\" tab.</p> \n<p><img alt=\"tiktok discover tab to find trends\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/TikTok%20Trends%20B2B%20and%20B2C%20Marketers%20Should%20Watch%20in%202022-1.jpeg?width=250&amp;name=TikTok%20Trends%20B2B%20and%20B2C%20Marketers%20Should%20Watch%20in%202022-1.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 250px;\" title=\"how to find tiktok trends: the discover tab\" width=\"250\"></p> \n<p>On this tab, you can scroll through popular sounds, hashtags, and topics along with a preview of the top videos within the category.</p> \n<p><img alt=\"tiktok discover tab to find trends\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/TikTok%20Trends%20B2B%20and%20B2C%20Marketers%20Should%20Watch%20in%202022-4.jpeg?width=250&amp;name=TikTok%20Trends%20B2B%20and%20B2C%20Marketers%20Should%20Watch%20in%202022-4.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; width: 250px; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" title=\"\" width=\"250\"></p> \n<p>You can also see how many videos fall within that category, which gives you an insight into which trends are rising and which ones have already blown up.</p> \n<h3>2. The \"For You\" Page</h3> \n<p>TikTok’s \"For You\" page is like Instagram’s Explore page. It looks different for every user based on the content they engage with the most.</p> \n<p>With that said, it’s also where trending topics make their rounds.</p> \n<p><img alt=\"tiktok for you page to find trends\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/TikTok%20Trends%20B2B%20and%20B2C%20Marketers%20Should%20Watch%20in%202022-2.jpeg?width=250&amp;name=TikTok%20Trends%20B2B%20and%20B2C%20Marketers%20Should%20Watch%20in%202022-2.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; width: 250px; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" title=\"\" width=\"250\"></p> \n<p>If a video has hundreds of thousands of likes or views, it’s worth digging a bit to see if it’s related to a particular trend. Your first step should be checking the sound, located on the bottom left corner of the video.</p> \n<p><img alt=\"tiktok for you page\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/TikTok%20Trends%20B2B%20and%20B2C%20Marketers%20Should%20Watch%20in%202022-3.jpeg?width=300&amp;name=TikTok%20Trends%20B2B%20and%20B2C%20Marketers%20Should%20Watch%20in%202022-3.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 300px;\" title=\"how to find tiktok trend for you page\" width=\"300\"></p> \n<p>Once you click on it, you’ll see the name of the song, the number of videos that use it, and scroll to see the videos that feature it. With all this information, you’ll know how popular a sound is and how other users are leveraging it.</p> \n<h3>3. The \"Search\" Tab</h3> \n<p>TikTok’s search tab is another great way to discover new trends.</p> \n<p>Before you start typing in the search bar, TikTok auto-populates suggested searches based on trending topics.</p> \n<p><img alt=\"tiktok search bar to find trends\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/TikTok%20Trends%20B2B%20and%20B2C%20Marketers%20Should%20Watch%20in%202022.jpeg?width=300&amp;name=TikTok%20Trends%20B2B%20and%20B2C%20Marketers%20Should%20Watch%20in%202022.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 300px;\" title=\"\" width=\"300\"></p> \n<p>All you have to do is then click on relevant searches and see what videos have been created surrounding these topics.</p> \n<h3>4. The #TrendAlert Hashtag</h3> \n<p>Now, let’s say you leverage all the strategies mentioned above and you’re still struggling to identify trends.</p> \n<p>Well, there are a ton of users on TikTok who are already on top of it. All you have to do is follow them or the hashtag #TrendAlert.</p> \n<blockquote class=\"tiktok-embed\" cite=\"https://www.tiktok.com/@strategisewithcare/video/7066856216848387334\" style=\"max-width: 605px; min-width: 325px;\"> \n <a title=\"@strategisewithcare\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/@strategisewithcare\">@strategisewithcare</a> \n <a title=\"socialmediamanageruk\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/socialmediamanageruk\">#socialmediamanageruk</a> \n <a title=\"trendalert\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/trendalert\">#trendalert</a> \n <a title=\"contentcreatortips\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/contentcreatortips\">#contentcreatortips</a> \n <a title=\"smallbusinesstips_\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/smallbusinesstips_\">#smallbusinesstips_</a> \n <a title=\"trendpredictions\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/trendpredictions\">#trendpredictions</a> \n <a title=\"trendingnow\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/trendingnow\">#trendingnow</a> \n <a title=\"tiktoktips\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/tiktoktips\">#tiktoktips</a> \n <a title=\"trendalert2022\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/trendalert2022\">#trendalert2022</a> \n <a title=\"contentideas\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/contentideas\">#contentideas</a> \n <a title=\"♬ original sound - Betelgeusethestar\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/music/original-sound-7064658646256651009\">♬ original sound - Betelgeusethestar</a> \n</blockquote>  \n<p>As shown in the video, you can leverage this hashtag to discover new trends and how to use them.</p> \n<h2>How to Do TikTok Trends</h2> \n<h3>1. Jump in early.</h3> \n<p>The thing about trends is that they come and go very quickly. If you don’t jump in early, you might miss the boat altogether.</p> \n<p>So, as soon as you identify a TikTok trend you want to participate in, start brainstorming some ideas.</p> \n<p>Keep in mind that you don’t need fancy videography to succeed on the platform. Often, all it takes is some creative thinking, good lighting, some lip-syncing skills, and a phone.</p> \n<p>Authenticity is essential on a platform like TikTok. If you keep that at the forefront, your odds of success are that much higher.</p> \n<h3>2. Find a relatable angle.</h3> \n<p>On TikTok, you only have up to three minutes to make an impression but a good chunk of videos that go viral are 30 seconds or less.</p> \n<p>This means you have a short ramp-up period to get viewers to stop and watch your video. One way to do this? Create relatable content.</p> \n<blockquote class=\"tiktok-embed\" cite=\"https://www.tiktok.com/@thelipbar/video/6826854225931193606\" style=\"max-width: 605px; min-width: 325px;\"> \n <a title=\"@thelipbar\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/@thelipbar\">@thelipbar</a> I mean... it’s hard to resist our \n <a title=\"fastface\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/fastface\">#fastface</a> makeup system 😍 \n <a title=\"thelipbar\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/thelipbar\">#thelipbar</a> \n <a title=\"easymakeup\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/easymakeup\">#easymakeup</a> \n <a title=\"vegan\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/vegan\">#vegan</a> \n <a title=\"vegancosmetics\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/vegancosmetics\">#vegancosmetics</a> \n <a title=\"fyp\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/fyp\">#fyp</a> \n <a title=\"foryou\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/tag/foryou\">#foryou</a> \n <a title=\"♬ original sound - Makayla\" href=\"https://www.tiktok.com/music/original-sound-6776283960856169222\">♬ original sound - Makayla</a> \n</blockquote>  \n<p>Think about the challenges your audience faces on a day-to-day. That’s a great place to get inspiration from.</p> \n<p>You can also get inspired by your competitors and the content they’re creating.</p> \n<h3>3. Know when to bow out.</h3> \n<p>Every day, there’s a new TikTok trend.</p> \n<p>With this in mind, not every trend is worth joining in. This could be because it doesn’t align with your brand voice and values, or because you missed the boat.</p> \n<p>Whatever the reason, avoid joining trends long after they’ve peaked. At that point, users may be over the trend and actively avoid it. It can also make your brand seem out of touch.</p> \n<p>TikTok trends are always evolving. If you leverage the tools mentioned here, you can join the trends as they happen and reach an ever-growing audience.</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/cs/ci/?pg=7a03a7b4-d90f-4c86-b845-fae9305669ea&amp;pid=53&amp;ecid=&amp;hseid=&amp;hsic=\"><img class=\"hs-cta-img \" style=\"border-width: 0px; /*hs-extra-styles*/; \" alt=\"Blog - Content Mapping Template\" src=\"https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/53/7a03a7b4-d90f-4c86-b845-fae9305669ea.png\"></a></p> \n<p></p>  \n<img src=\"https://track.hubspot.com/__ptq.gif?a=53&amp;k=14&amp;r=https%3A%2F%2Fblog.hubspot.com%2Fmarketing%2Ftiktok-trends&amp;bu=https%253A%252F%252Fblog.hubspot.com%252Fmarketing&amp;bvt=rss\"
