16:15:05","updatedTime":"2022-03-14 16:15:05","title":"What is Content Governance? 4 Easy Steps to Create a Model in 2022","link":"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/content-governance-model","description":"<p>Without a content governance model in place, your <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/content-marketing\">content marketing</a> efforts can seem scattered and chaotic, opening the opportunity for your audience to replace you with a competitor.</p> \n<p></p> \n<p>Content governance keeps your relationship with your customers thriving, and allows you and your team to more effectively focus on your content goals.</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/cs/ci/?pg=a145a75e-59f6-4b51-a482-4f3ea486e740&amp;pid=53&amp;ecid=&amp;hseid=&amp;hsic=\"><img class=\"hs-cta-img \" style=\"border-width: 0px; /*hs-extra-styles*/; margin: 0 auto; display: block; margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px\" alt=\"Free Resource: Content Marketing Planning Template\" src=\"https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/53/a145a75e-59f6-4b51-a482-4f3ea486e740.png\" align=\"middle\"></a></p> \n<p>In this post, we’ll cover the topic of content governance — what it is, why it’s important, and how you can create a model for your business.</p> \n<p></p> \n<p>The goal of a <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/content-marketing-plan\">content strategy</a> is for your company to create meaningful and engaging content that aligns with your business objectives and drives consumers to a particular action. Content governance ensures that you have a definitive way for this content to reach them. Who creates the content? On what platform is it published? How will it be updated in the future? While these questions and their answers help shape content governance, its framework involves more.</p> \n<p>Content governance is more than consumer-facing content. It requires preliminary and behind-the-scenes work seen in an asset like an <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/business-blog-editorial-calendar-templates\">editorial content calendar</a>. Consumers don’t have access to your company’s content calendar; however, this is an irreplaceable tool to keep your company on track with its strategy. <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/blog/tabid/6307/bid/31247/the-simple-template-for-a-thorough-content-style-guide.aspx\">Style guides</a> and <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/company-content-audit\">content audits</a> are other tools that assist with content governance but are unseen by consumers.</p> \n<p>Content governance encompasses content sent to consumers and content that waits for them. It is not only reserved for social media posts that land on their feed or emails sent to their inbox. It includes banner ads or frequently asked questions on your website. It’s your Instagram bio or the answering message you have for phone calls. In a business, content is <em>everywhere</em>, and content governance allows your business to manage all of its avenues.</p> \n<h2>Why is content governance important?</h2> \n<p>To illustrate the importance of content governance, let’s look at an analogy.</p> \n<p>Content marketing is like a first date. You wine and dine with visuals and information and hope it builds a budding relationship. If it does, how do you move forward and keep building?</p> \n<p>After that initial interaction, you publish two emails, one blog post, and four social media posts during week one. You drop the ball in week two. The amount of content decreases to one email and two social media posts. Week three is worse, but during week four, you’re able to publish three emails, two blog posts, and five social media posts. While the increase in content <em>seems</em> remarkable, your potential long-term customer has unsubscribed from your content after a month. Why?</p> \n<p><em>Content</em> needs to be <em>governed</em> by procedures and systems. Procedures mean consistency, and consistency is key to the success of any business. It shows effort and demonstrates to customers that you <em>care</em>.</p> \n<p>Content works as a cycle. Although the number of steps might differ for each organization, content life cycles typically follow this process:</p> \n<ul> \n <li>Develop a strategy.</li> \n <li>Create the content.</li> \n <li>Store the content.</li> \n <li>Edit.</li> \n <li>Publish.</li> \n <li>Analyze.</li> \n <li>Update or repurpose content.</li> \n</ul> \n<p>The content cycle never ends. There is always work to do. Use the steps above. If you finish strategizing, focus on content creation. If you’re not creating, your company can work on storing, editing, publishing, and more.</p> \n<p>Content governance is important because it ensures that your company maintains an efficient process in its continuous content cycle. It can prevent delays, inconsistent messaging, or even legal issues. Content governance helps:</p> \n<ul> \n <li>Provide structure</li> \n <li>Establish clear roles and responsibilities</li> \n <li>Create detailed processes and workflows</li> \n <li>Outline company standards and policies</li> \n</ul> \n<p>A comprehensive content governance model creates a standard for effective, consistent content, resulting in continued success.</p> \n<p>The online world is fast-paced, and to keep up, businesses need to make sure that they’re covering all avenues. It used to mean website and email content; however, the growth of social media has expanded the number of channels businesses need to account for. Companies have had to shift gears and adjust their content strategies to accommodate social platforms like Facebook, Instagram, and LinkedIn.</p> \n<p>While content grows and changes, its governance models help companies scale, sustain, and recreate their content.</p> \n<h2>Creating a Content Governance Model</h2> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/content-governance-models.png?width=650&amp;name=content-governance-models.png\" alt=\"content governance model components\" width=\"650\" style=\"width: 650px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<p>You’re ready to create your content governance model. While each step might require extensive work, the process isn’t complicated. Building your content governance model requires four steps.</p> \n<ul> \n <li>Establish and define the roles and responsibilities of the content team.</li> \n <li>Design content workflows.</li> \n <li>Create policies, standards, and procedures for content.</li> \n <li>Document guidelines and ensure company-wide compliance.</li> \n</ul> \n<p>Let's go over these one-by-one.</p> \n<h3>1. Establish and define the roles and responsibilities of the content team.</h3> \n<p>Good content doesn’t exist without people. While you could argue that the most vital person in the content experience is the consumer, you could also contend that content would not exist without the team.</p> \n<p>To create a content governance model, decide on the roles and responsibilities of those within the company. Content roles include strategists, writers, editors, and analysts. When defining the obligations of the people in these roles, think about their function. Team members typically have a strategic, operational, or specialist function.</p> \n<p>A strategic function, usually seen in roles like a content strategist, is for those who plan long-term strategy. Staff, who are operational, implement the content strategy daily. This work is carried out by writers, editors, photographers, and more. Lastly, members of the specialist function provide expert data to other team members. This could be an SEO specialist providing analytical information to strategists or writers that shape how they fulfill their role.</p> \n<p>When establishing the roles and responsibilities for your team, you might find it necessary to create an overlap in function. For example, it could be beneficial to have your content writers specialize in SEO. As long as there is a clear distinction in role and responsibility, there should be no issue in team management.</p> \n<h3>2. Design content workflows.</h3> \n<p>How does your content go from Point A to Point B? Point A is an idea while Point B is publication. Consumers cannot see this process, but multiple steps are necessary to reach publication.</p> \n<p>Content workflows follow these stages:</p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/content-marketing-plan\"><strong>Strategy</strong></a><strong>:</strong> planning content</li> \n <li><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/content-creation\"><strong>Creation</strong></a><strong>:</strong> writing, designing, filming, content</li> \n <li><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/ultimate-editing-checklist\"><strong>Review</strong></a><strong>:</strong> editing and fact-checking content</li> \n <li><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/content-distribution\"><strong>Publication/Distribution</strong></a><strong>:</strong> publishing and sharing content</li> \n</ul> \n<p>While the list is short, the process isn’t. Content takes time. Once you’re aware of what it takes to create your content, use this to shape your policies, standards, and procedures.</p> \n<h3>3. Create policies, standards, and procedures for content.</h3> \n<p>Once you have the proper people in place, it is time to focus on your policies, standards, and procedures. Content policies are the values and goals of a company. Standards are targets used to make sure that a company upholds its policies. Procedures are a step-by-step breakdown of who is involved and what steps are needed to achieve the ultimate goal.</p> \n<p>Consider this example. An online company has the <strong>policy</strong> to be a leading source of global news. The company enforces this policy by setting a <strong>standard</strong> for publishing at least 10 daily articles. Members of the content team, like the writers, editors, and publishers, have <strong>procedures</strong> to guide them through the content process and ensure that 10 articles are shared with the public every day.</p> \n<p>Once your company creates policies, standards, and procedures for content, finish the process with documentation and compliance.</p> \n<h3>4. Document guidelines and ensure company-wide compliance.</h3> \n<p>There is no use in creating a content governance model if no one knows about it. The most significant element of content governance is ensuring that the entire company has access to it and complies with it.</p> \n<p>Create documents for your company policies, standards, and procedures, and put them in a central location. Hold a meeting to walk through content processes and workflows. And lastly, regularly review and update your content governance models.</p> \n<h2>Content never ends.</h2> \n<p>Content lives on a lifecycle. You might think a blog post is complete after it is published and distributed, but its cycle continues with updates and redistribution. Managing one blog post without a system is most likely doable, but imagine an additional 20 content assets in one week. Scary, right?</p> \n<p>Without any checks and balances, creating and managing your content can become chaotic. Content governance prevents this. With a content governance model in place, your company will have the framework and processes in place to successfully execute your content strategy.</p> \n<p></p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" margin: 0 auto; display: block; margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px\" alt=\"Blog - Content Mapping Template\" MailChimp</h3> \n<p>Best for actionable data insights to improve your email marketing strategy.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Mailchimp.jpg?width=1264&amp;name=Mailchimp.jpg\" alt=\"Mailchimp email marketing platform\" width=\"1264\" style=\"width: 1264px;\">Over the years, <a href=\"https://mailchimp.com/\">MailChimp</a> has added landing pages and various ads tools to their capabilities but, their email marketing service remains their claim-to-fame.</p> \n<h4>MailChimp Features</h4> \n<p>MailChimp has millions of customers in over 175 countries and they use the data they collect off those customers to provide you with actionable insights to improve your email strategy. By using these integrations to further personalize your marketing, you'll get the most out of your email strategy.</p> \n<h4>MailChimp Price</h4> \n<p>MailChimp has <a href=\"https://mailchimp.com/pricing/\">four plans</a> to choose from that range in price from free to $299 per month. Aside from the free plan, depending on the option you go with, your monthly payment increases with the number of contacts you have.</p> \n<h3>11. AWeber</h3> \n<p>Best for small businesses and entrepreneurs just starting to build their email lists.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/AWeber.jpg?width=1255&amp;name=AWeber.jpg\" alt=\"AWeber email marketing platform\" width=\"1255\" style=\"width: 1255px;\"><a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/\">Aweber</a> is an email platform built specifically for small businesses and entrepreneurs.</p> \n<h4>AWeber Features</h4> \n<p>The goal of AWeber is to make it simple for those who are just getting started with email marketing to segment their contacts, design a professional email, and start nurturing leads. Customers have praised AWeber for its deliverability — AWeber's deliverability team monitors their servers around the clock to ensure your campaign consistently reaches the' inboxes of your recipients.</p> \n<h4>Aweber Price</h4> \n<p>AWeber offers <a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/pricing.htm\">two plans</a>: free and pro. The AWeber Pro plan starts at $16.15 per month, and increases in price depending on the size of your list. You can also choose to pay on a quarterly or annual cycle if that's preferred over monthly billing.</p> \n<h3>12. ActiveCampaign</h3> \n<p>Best for segmentation and live chat options.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/ActiveCampaign.jpg?width=1253&amp;name=ActiveCampaign.jpg\" alt=\"ActiveCampaign\" width=\"1253\" style=\"width: 1253px;\"><a href=\"https://www.activecampaign.com\">ActiveCampaign</a> is a marketing automation platform that offers <a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/products/crm/live-chat?_ga=2.262995208.567721879.1555430872-644648569.1551722047\">live chat</a> and a <a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/products/crm?_ga=2.95719576.567721879.1555430872-644648569.1551722047\">CRM service</a> in addition to email marketing capabilities.</p> \n<h4>ActiveCampaign Features</h4> \n<p>By adding a CRM to their functionality, ActiveCampaign can help surface the right leads to your sales team using features like lead scoring. The service also allows you to share dynamic content in your emails — this allows you to provide different experiences to your contacts based on the way you segment them.</p> \n<h4>ActiveCampaign Price</h4> \n<p>ActiveCampaign has <a href=\"https://www.activecampaign.com/pricing/\">four plans</a> which you can choose to pay for monthly or annually. Their plans vary based on the number of contacts you have and range in price from $9 to $259. You can experiment with the service before buying it with a free trial, as well.</p> \n<h3>13. AutoPilot</h3> \n<p>Best for collaborative email marketing teams.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Autopilot.jpg?width=1263&amp;name=Autopilot.jpg\" alt=\"Autopilot email marketing platform\" width=\"1263\" style=\"width: 1263px;\"><a href=\"https://www.autopilothq.com/\">Autopilot</a> differentiates themselves from the competitors with their visual marketing tools.</p> \n<h4>AutoPilot Features</h4> \n<p>Everything from AutoPilot's email editor to their automation tool is set up to work via a drag-and-drop interface, making the system intuitive and easy to use.</p> \n<p>AutoPilot offers collaborative tools to help your team work together effectively — it allows you to quickly share your work with your team, ensuring everyone is on the same page before you launch a campaign. And with the \"annotate &amp; collaborate\" feature, you can quickly mark-up a customer journey and ask your team for feedback and assistance.</p> \n<h4>AutoPilot Price</h4> \n<p>AutoPilot offers <a href=\"https://www.autopilothq.com/pricing\">three plans</a> which range in price between $49 and $249 that vary based on your number of contacts. There are three types of billing cycles including monthly, monthly with an annual commitment, and annual.</p> \n<h3>14. GetResponse</h3> \n<p>Best for global email marketing audiences.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/GetResponse.jpg?width=1258&amp;name=GetResponse.jpg\" alt=\"GetResponse email marketing platform\" width=\"1258\" style=\"width: 1258px;\"><a href=\"https://www.getresponse.com/\">GetResponse</a> is a marketing automation service that's available in over 20 languages.</p> \n<h4>GetResponse Features</h4> \n<p>On top of email marketing and automation, GetResponse also offers a CRM, landing pages, and a complete webinar solution.</p> \n<p>The service offers over 500 templates to help you get started with email marketing and integrates with Shutterstock, giving you access to a creative library at your fingertips. Also, their drip campaign tool is managed through a calendar interface, allowing you to see exactly when you will be reaching out to your leads.</p> \n<h4>GetResponse Price</h4> \n<p>There are <a href=\"https://secure.getresponse.com/pricing/en\">four GetResponse plans</a> that you can choose from ranging in price from $15 to $99 per month (plus a customized enterprise-level option that requires you to reach out for a quote). Pricing varies based on your list size and you can pay monthly or annually. Each plan offers a free trial so you can test out the service before investing.</p> \n<h3>15. Ontraport</h3> \n<p>Best for creating detailed email marketing campaigns.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Ontraport.jpg?width=1265&amp;name=Ontraport.jpg\" alt=\"Ontraport email marketing platform\" width=\"1265\" style=\"width: 1265px;\"><a href=\"https://ontraport.com/\">Ontraport</a> offers a full suite of marketing automation tools including ecommerce functionality for businesses with online stores.</p> \n<h4>Ontraport Features</h4> \n<p>Ontraport's visual campaign builder allows you to create detailed campaigns to engage your audience. You can create a campaign from scratch or tap into the marketplace where they offer dozens of the most common marketing campaigns to choose from, including abandoned cart nurturing or webinar sign-up and follow-up.</p> \n<p>The service also provides insight into detailed reports so you can gain insight into your pipeline, traffic sources, and conversion timelines.</p> \n<h4>Ontraport Price</h4> \n<p>Ontraport offers <a href=\"https://ontraport.com/pricing\">four plans</a> that range in price between $79 and $497 per month. No matter which plan you choose, you'll receive one-on-one onboarding. The plans differ in price based on your number of contacts. You can cancel your monthly plan at any time and if you choose to pay annually, you'll benefit from a discount.</p> \n<h3>16. Flodesk</h3> \n<p>Best for creating visually appealing emails and landing pages from easy-to-use templates.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Flodesk.jpg?width=1252&amp;name=Flodesk.jpg\" alt=\"Flodesk email marketing platform\" width=\"1252\" style=\"width: 1252px;\"></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://flodesk.com/\">Flodesk</a> is an affordable email provider that makes creating beautiful branded emails simple and easy.</p> \n<h4>Flodesk Features</h4> \n<p>Flodesk’s email building tools are intuitive and easy to use for beginners and email marketing experts alike. For those with creative businesses or strong visual brands, Flodesk works like a design tool to craft on-brand emails and landing pages.</p> \n<p>Flodesk also offers tagging and workflow options that make creating email automations a straightforward process, and integrations with tools such as Zapier and Shopify to streamline the different areas of your business.</p> \n<h4>Flodesk Price</h4> \n<p>Flodesk offers one plan with unlimited emails and contacts for a flat fee of <a href=\"https://flodesk.com/pricing.html\"><span>$38 per month</span></a>. For annual subscribers, Flodesk costs $418 per year. Users can try Flodesk for free for 30 days.</p> \n<h2>Choose Your Email Marketing Service</h2> \n<p>Most email marketing tools offer the essentials needed to craft a basic email newsletter, but there are fewer options if you want a range of top-notch features such as complete customization, available support, <em>and</em> data analysis.</p> \n<p>Not to mention, as a marketer, you might want to consider combining your <a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/products/marketing/email\">email marketing service</a> with a <a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/products/crm\">CRM</a> to give you even greater functionality that can impact your email marketing as well as other marketing sales, and service efforts. But. ultimately, the best email marketing tool for you depends on your team's goals and particular needs — so, review the options above as well as the services' product and pricing pages to get started.</p> \n<p><em>Editor's note: This post was originally published in April, 2019 and has been updated for comprehensiveness.</em></p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" 16:15:05","updatedTime":"2022-03-14 16:15:05","title":"How-To: Conditional Formatting Based on Another Cell in Google Sheets","link":"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/conditional-formatting-google-sheets","description":"<p>Conditional formatting is a feature in <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/google-sheets\">Google Sheets</a> in which a cell is formatted in a particular way when certain conditions are met. The formatting can include highlighting, bolding, italicizing – just about any visual changes to the cell.</p> \n<p>Just as it can be done for the cell you’re currently in, conditional formatting can also be set based on conditions met in another cell.</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/cs/ci/?pg=e7cd3f82-cab9-4017-b019-ee3fc550e0b5&amp;pid=53&amp;ecid=&amp;hseid=&amp;hsic=\"><img class=\"hs-cta-img \" style=\"border-width: 0px; /*hs-extra-styles*/; \" alt=\"→ Access Now: Google Sheets Templates [Free Kit]\" src=\"https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/53/e7cd3f82-cab9-4017-b019-ee3fc550e0b5.png\"></a></p> \n<p>Let’s dive into how to create this condition based on multiple criteria.</p> \n<h2>How Conditional Formatting Works</h2> \n<p>To learn how to set conditional formatting, let’s use this workbook as an example.</p> \n<p><img alt=\"example of a google sheets workbook to show how conditional formatting works \" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-3.jpeg?width=600&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-3.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 600px;\" title=\"\" width=\"600\"></p> \n<p>It’s a workbook showing website traffic year over year from Q4 2020 to Q4 2021, with the page views along with the year-over-year percentage change.</p> \n<p>Here’s what we want to accomplish here: When the percentage change is positive YoY, the cell turns green. When it’s negative, the cell turns red. This makes it easy to get a quick performance overview before diving into the details.</p> \n<p>Here are the steps to set the conditional formatting.</p> \n<h3>1. Select the cell you want to format, click on \"Format\" from the navigation bar, then click on \"Conditional Formatting.\"</h3> \n<h3 style=\"font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-family: AvenirNext, 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; color: #33475b;\"><img alt=\"how to set the conditional formatting step 1 \" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-Feb-11-2022-04-54-48-47-PM.jpeg?width=600&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-Feb-11-2022-04-54-48-47-PM.jpeg\" title=\"\" width=\"600\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 600px;\"></h3> \n<br> \n<h3>2. While staying in the \"Single color\" tab, double-check that the cell under \"Apply to range\" is the cell you want to format. <img alt=\"how to set the conditional formatting step 2\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-3.png?width=250&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-3.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 250px;\" title=\"\" width=\"250\"></h3> \n<br> \n<h3>3. Set your format rules.</h3> \n<img alt=\"how to set the conditional formatting step 3\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets.png?width=250&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets.png\" title=\"\" width=\"250\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 250px;\"> \n<p>It may automatically default to a standard conditional formatting formula. In this case, open the dropdown menu under \"Format cells if…\" to select your rules. Options will look as follows:</p> \n<h3>4. <span style=\"font-size: 1.5rem; font-weight: 500;\">Choose your formatting style, then click \"Done.\"</span><img alt=\"how to set the conditional formatting step 4\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-1.png?width=250&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-1.png\" title=\"\" width=\"250\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 250px;\"></h3> \n<h3>5. Confirm the rule was applied under \"Conditional Formatting Rules.\"</h3> \n<img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/conditional%20formatting%20step%205-png.png?width=250&amp;name=conditional%20formatting%20step%205-png.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 250px;\" width=\"250\" alt=\"conditional formatting step 5\"> \n<h3>6. Add another rule if needed.</h3> \n<img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/conditional%20formatting%20step%206-png.png?width=200&amp;name=conditional%20formatting%20step%206-png.png\" width=\"200\" style=\"width: 200px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" alt=\"conditional formatting step 6\">\n<br> \n<h3>7. Return to cell to view formatting, then drag the cursor to apply to other cells, if needed.</h3> \n<img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/conditional%20formatting%20step%207-gif.gif?width=600&amp;name=conditional%20formatting%20step%207-gif.gif\" alt=\"how to set the conditional formatting step 7\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 600px;\" width=\"600\"> \n<p>Now that you understand the basics, let’s cover how to use conditional formatting based on other cells.</p> \n<h2>Conditional Formatting Based on Another Cell Value</h2> \n<h3>1. Select the cell you want to format.</h3> \n<p><img alt=\"conditional formatting based on another cell value step 1\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets.jpeg?width=600&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 600px;\" title=\"\" width=\"600\"></p> \n<h3>2. Click on \"Format\" in the navigation bar, then select \"Conditional Formatting.\"</h3> \n<p><img alt=\"conditional formatting based on another cell value step 2\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-Feb-11-2022-04-54-50-23-PM.jpeg?width=250&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-Feb-11-2022-04-54-50-23-PM.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; width: 250px; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" title=\"\" width=\"250\"></p> \n<h3>3. Under \"Format Rules,\" select \"Custom formula is.\"</h3> \n<p><img alt=\"conditional formatting based on another cell value step 3\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-Feb-11-2022-04-54-49-26-PM.jpeg?width=200&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-Feb-11-2022-04-54-49-26-PM.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 200px;\" title=\"\" width=\"200\"></p> \n<h3>4. Write your formula, then click \"Done.\"</h3> \n<p><img alt=\"conditional formatting based on another cell value step 4\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-4.png?width=200&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-4.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 200px;\" title=\"\" width=\"200\"></p> \n<h3>5. Confirm your rule has been applied and check the cell.</h3> \n<p><img alt=\"conditional formatting based on another cell value step 5\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-Feb-11-2022-04-54-48-82-PM.jpeg?width=600&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-Feb-11-2022-04-54-48-82-PM.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 600px;\" title=\"\" width=\"600\"></p> \n<h2>Conditional Formatting Based on Another Cell Range</h2> \n<p>To format based on another cell range, you follow many of the same steps you would for a cell value. What changes is the formula you write.</p> \n<h3>1. Select the cell you want to format.</h3> \n<p><img alt=\"conditional formatting based on another cell range step 1\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-2.jpeg?width=624&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-2.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" title=\"\" width=\"624\"></p> \n<h3>2. Click on \"Format\" in the navigation bar, then select \"Conditional Formatting.\"</h3> \n<p><img alt=\"conditional formatting based on another cell range step 2\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-4.jpeg?width=350&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-4.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 350px;\" title=\"\" width=\"350\"></p> \n<h3>3. Under \"Format Rules,\" select \"Custom formula is.\"</h3> \n<p><img alt=\"conditional formatting based on another cell range step 3\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-Feb-11-2022-04-54-49-26-PM.jpeg?width=200&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-Feb-11-2022-04-54-49-26-PM.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 200px;\" title=\"\" width=\"200\"></p> \n<h3>4. Write your formula using the following format: <strong>=value range &lt; [value], </strong>select your formatting style, then click \"Done.\"</h3> \n<p><img alt=\"conditional formatting based on another cell range step 4\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-Feb-11-2022-04-54-50-58-PM.png?width=200&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-Feb-11-2022-04-54-50-58-PM.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; width: 200px; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" title=\"\" width=\"200\"></p> \n<h3>5. Confirm your rule has been applied and check the cell.</h3> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20Range%20step%205-jpg.jpeg?width=600&amp;name=Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20Range%20step%205-jpg.jpeg\" width=\"600\" style=\"width: 600px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" alt=\"conditional formatting based on another cell range step 5\"></p> \n<p></p> \n<h2>Google Sheets Conditional Formatting Based on Another Cell Color</h2> \n<p>Currently, <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/google-sheets-templates\">Google Sheets </a>does not offer a way to use conditional formatting based on the color of another cell. You can only use it based on:</p> \n<ul> \n <li><strong>Values</strong> – higher than, greater than, equal to, in between</li> \n <li><strong>Text</strong> – contains, starts with, ends with, matches</li> \n <li><strong>Dates</strong> – is before, is after, is exactly</li> \n <li><strong>Emptiness</strong> – is empty, is not empty</li> \n</ul> \n<p>To achieve your goal, you’d have to use the condition of the cell to format the other.</p> \n<p>Let’s use an example.</p> \n<p><img alt=\"Google Sheets Conditional Formatting Based on Another Cell Color\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-1.jpeg?width=600&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-1.jpeg\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 600px;\" title=\"\" width=\"600\"></p> \n<p>Say you want to format cell A2 (September 2020) to be red and match the color of cell E2 (-20%). There’s no formula that allows you to create a condition based on color. However, you can create a custom formula based on E2’s values.</p> \n<p>You can say that if cell E2’s values are less than 0, cell A2 turns red. The formula is as follows: <strong>= [The other cell] &lt; [value].</strong> In this case, the formula would be =e2&lt;0, as it signifies that cell A2 should turn red if E2’s value is less than 0.</p> \n<p><img alt=\"google sheets conditional formatting based on another cell's values\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-2.png?width=200&amp;name=How%20to%20Set%20Conditional%20Formatting%20Based%20on%20Another%20Cell%20in%20Google%20Sheets-2.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; width: 200px; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" title=\"\" width=\"200\"></p> \n<p>With so many functions to play with, Google Sheets can seem daunting. By following these simple steps, you can easily format your cells for quick scanning.</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/cs/ci/?pg=0cedc81d-d358-4517-bd55-4a26f49c5a4e&amp;pid=53&amp;ecid=&amp;hseid=&amp;hsic=\"><img class=\"hs-cta-img \" style=\"border-width: 0px; /*hs-extra-styles*/; \" alt=\"business google sheets templates\" src=\"https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/53/0cedc81d-d358-4517-bd55-4a26f49c5a4e.png\"></a></p> \n<p></p>  \n<img
